The date should match the format "dd/mm/yyyy". The day should be between 01 and 31, the month should be between 01 and 12, and the year should be a four-digit number between 0001 and 9999. The month of February should also account for leap years, so it should allow the date 29/02/yyyy only if the year is a leap year.

1. The first three characters are the consonants of the surname.

Based on the Wikipedia description, the Unique Master Citizen Number (UMCN) in Serbia has the following format:
11 digits in the format DDMMLLFFFXYC, where:
- DD represents the day of birth (01-31)
- MM represents the month of birth (01-12)
- LL represents the last two digits of the birth year (00-99)
^(?:[0-9]{1,3}(?:\.[0-9]{1,3})?|1000(?:\.0{1,3})?)$
^[A-Za-z][A-Za-z'- ]*[A-Za-z]$
Explanation of the regex:
- ^ : Start of the string
- [A-Za-z] : Matches any uppercase or lowercase letter
- [A-Za-z'- ]* : Matches zero or more occurrences of uppercase or lowercase letters, hyphens, apostrophes, or spaces
- [A-Za-z] : Matches any uppercase or lowercase letter
- $ : End of the string

- `\bsnake\b` - matches the exact word "snake"
- `\bhiss\w*` - matches words starting with "hiss" such as "hiss", "hisses", "hissing", etc.
- `\bnoise\b` - matches the exact word "noise"
- `\bof\b` - matches the exact word "of"
- `\ba\b` - matches the exact word "a"
Putting it all together:
`\bsnake\b.*\bhiss\w*.*\bnoise\b.*\bof\b\s*\ba\b`
